\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The \mbox{\hyperlink{classUniverse_1_1IUniverseCspSolver}{IUniverse\+Csp\+Solver}} interface defines the contract for CSP solvers.

{\em forbidden\+Values} & The values forbidden for the tuple variables. Values equal to null are interpreted as \char`\"{}any value\char`\"{} (as in so-\/called \char`\"{}starred tuples\char`\"{}).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
